tathA vAyavyasharIrArambhe vAyumayo bhavati /
tathA'kAshasharIrArambha AkAshamayo bhavati /
evametAni taijasAni devasharIrANi /
teShvArabhyamANeShu tanmayastejomayo bhavati /
ato vyatiriktAni pashvAdisharIrANi narakapretAdisharIrANi cAtejomayAni tAnyapekShyA'hAtejomaya iti /
evaM kAryakaraNasaMghAtamayaH sannAtmA prAptavyaM vastvantaraM pashyannidaM mayA prAptamado mayA prAptavyamityevaM viparItapratyayastadabhilAShaH kAmamayo bhavati /
tasminkAme doShaM pashyatastadviShayAbhilAShaprashAme citaM prasannamakaluShaM shAntaM bhavati /
tanmayo 'kAmamayaH /

iti smaraNAt /

kiM bahunA tadetatsidvamasya yadayamidaMmayo gR^ihyamANaviShayAdidaMmayastasmAdayamadomayaH /
ada iti parokShaM kAryeNa gR^ihyamANena nirdishyate /
anantA hyantaHkaraNe bhAvanAvisheShAH /
naiva te visheShato nirdeShTuM shakyante /
tasmistasminkShaNe kAryato 'vagamyanta idamasya hradi vartate 'dosyate tena gR^ihyamANakAryeNedaMmayatayA nirdishyate parokSho 'ntaHstho vyavahAro 'yamidAnImadomaya iti /
saMkShepatastu yathA kartuM yathA vA carituM shIlamasya so 'yaM yathAkArI yathA cArI sa tathA bhavati /
karaNaM nAma niyatA kriyA vidhipratiShedhAdigamyA caraNaM nAmAniyatamiti visheShaH /
sAdhukArI sAdhurbhavatIti yathAkArItyasya visheShaNaM pApakArI pApo bhavatIti ca yathAcArItyasya /
tAcchIlyapratyayopAdAnAdatyantatAtparyataiva tanmayatvaM na tu tatkarmamAtreNotyAshaN^kayA'ha-puNyaH puNyena karmaNA bhavati pApaH pApeneti /
puNyapApakarmamAtreNaiva tanmayatA syAnna tu tAcchIlyamapekShate /

tasmAtpuNyApuNye saMsArasya kAraNam /

upacite api puNyapuNye karmaNI kAmashUnye phalArambhake na bhavataH /

kraturnAdhyavasAyo nishcayo yadanantarA kriyA pravartate /

yatkarma kurute tadabhisaMpadyate, tadIyaM phalamabhisaMpadyate /
tasmAtsarvamayatve 'sya saMsAritve ca kAma heturiti //4,4.5//

START BrhUp 4,4.6

#<tad eSha shloko bhavati --
tad eva saktaH saha karmaNaiti liN^gaM mano yatra niShaktam asya |
prApyAntaM karmaNas tasya yat kiJNceha karoty ayam |
tasmAl lokAt punar aity asmai lokAya karmaNe |
iti nu kAmayamAnaH |
athAkAmayamAno yo 'kAmo niShkAma AptakAma AtmakAmo na tasya prANA utkrAmanti |
brahmaiva san brahmApyeti || BrhUp_4,4.6 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_4,4.6 tattasminnartha eSha shloko mantropi bhavati /
tadevaiti tadeva gacchati sakta AsaktastatrodbhUtAbhilAShaH sannityarthaH /
kathameti /
saha karmaNA yatkarmaphalAsaktaH sannakarottena karmaNA sahaiva tadeti tatphalameti /
kiM talliN^gamanaH /
manaH pradhAnatvAlliN^gasya mano liN^gamityucyate /
athavA liN^gayate 'vagamyate 'vagacchati yena talliN^gaM tanmano yatra yasminniShaktaM nishcayena saktamudbhUtAbhilAShamasya saMsAriNaH /
tadabhilASho hi tatkarma kR^itavAn /
tasmAttanmano 'bhiShaN^gavashAdevAsya tena karmaNA tatphalaprAptiH /
tenaitasidvaM bhavati kAmo mUlaM saMsArasyeti /
ata ucchinnakAmasya vidyamAnAnyapi karmANi brahmavido vandhyaprasavAni bhavanti /
"paryAptakAmasaya kR^itAtmanashca ihaiva sarve pravilItanti kAmAH"iti shruteH /
kiJNca prApyAntaM karmaNaH prApya bhuktvAntamavasAnaM tasya karmaNaH phalaM bhuktvAntaM prApya tasmAllokAtpunaraityAgacchatyasmai lokAya karmaNe 'yaM hi lokaH karmapradhAnastenA'ha karmaNa iti /
punaH karmakaraNAya punaH karma kR^itvA phalAsaN^gavashAtpunaramuM lokaM yAtItyevam /
iti nvevaM nu kAmayamAnaH saMsarati /
ya mAtkAmayamAna evaivaM saMsaratyatha tasmAdakAmayamAno na kvacitsaMsarati /
phalAsaktasya hi gatiruktA /
akAmasya hi kriyAnupapatterakAmayamAno mucyata eva /
kathaM punakAmayamAno bhavati /
yo 'kAmo bhavatyasAvakAmayamAnaH kathamakAmatetyucyate--yo niShTakAmo yasmAnnirgatAH kAmAH so 'yaM niShkAmaH /
kathaM kAmA nirgacchanti /
ya AptakAmo bhavatyAptAH kAmA yena sa AptakAmaH /
kathamApyante kAmA AtmakAmatvena yasyA'maiva nAnyaH kAmayitavyo vastvantarabhUtaH padArtho bhavati /
AtmaivAnantaro 'bAhyaH kR^itsnaH praj~nAnaghana ekaraso nordhva na tiryaÇnAdha Atmano 'nyatkAmayitavyaM vastvantaram /
yasya sarvamAtmaivAbhUttatkena kaM pashyecchR^iNuyAnmanvIta vijAnIyAdvaivaM vijAnankaM kAmayeta /
j~nAyamAno hyanyatvena padArthaH kAmayitavyo bhavati /
na cAsAvanyo brahmavida AptakAmasyAsti /
ya evA'tmakAmatayA'ptakAmaH sa niShkAmo 'kAmo 'kAmayamAnashceti mucyate /
na hi yasyA'tmaiva sarvaM bhavati tasyAnAtmA kAmayitavyo 'sti /
anAtmA cAnyaH kAmayitavyaH sarvaM cA'tmaivAbhUditi vipratiShidvam /
sarvAtmadarshinaH kAmayitavyAbhAvAtkarmAnupapattiH /
ye tu pratyavAyaparihArArthaM karma kalpayanti brahmavido 'pi teShAM sarva bhavati /
pratyavAyasya jihAsitavyasyA'tmano 'nyasyAbhipretatvAt /
yena cAshanAyAdyatIto nityaM pratyavAyasaMbadvo vidita AtmA taM vayaM brahmavidaM brUmaH /
nityamevAshanAyAdyatItamAtmanaM pashyati /
yasmAcca jihAsitavyamanyamupAdeyaM vA yo na pashyati tasya karma na shakyata eva saMbaddhu m /
yastvabrahmavitasya bhavatyeva pratyavAyaparihArArthaM karmeti na virodhaH /
ataH kAmAbhAvAdakAmayamAno na jAyate mucyata eva /
tasyaivamakAmayamAnasya karmAbhAve gamanakAraNAbhAvAtprANA vAgAdayo notkrAmanti nordhva krAmanti dehAt /
sa ca vidvAnAptakAma AtmakAmatayehaiva brahmabhUtaH /
sarvAtmano hi brahmaNo dR^iShTAntatvena pradarshitametadrUpaM tadvA asyaitadAptakAmamAtmakAmamakAmaM rUpamiti /
tasya hi dArShTAntikabhUto 'yamartha upasaMhriyate 'thAkAmayamAna ityAdinA /
sa kathamevaMbhUto mucyata ityucyate-yo hi suShuptAvasthamiva nirvisheShamadvaitamaluptacidrUpajyotiH svabhAvamAtmAnaM pashyati tasyaivAkAmayamAnasya karmabhAve gamanakAraNabhAvatprANA vAgAdayo notkrAmanti /
kintu vidvAnsaihaiva brahma, yadyapi dehAvAniva lakShyate sa brahmaiva sanbrahmApyeti /
yasmAnna hi tasyAbrahmatvaparicchedahetavaH kAmAH santi tasmAdihaiva brahmaiva sanbrahmApyeti na sharIrapAtettarakAlam /
na hi viduSho mR^itasya bhAvAntarApattirjIvato 'nyabhAvo dehAntarapratisaMdhAnAbhAvamAtreNova tu brahmApyetItyucyate /
bhAvAntarArApattau hi mokShasya sarvopaniShanidvivakShitor'tha AtmaikatvAkhyaH sa bAdhito bhavet /
karmahetukashca mokShaH prApnoti na j~nAnanimitta iti /
sa   cAniShTo 'nityatvaM ca mokShasya prApnoti /
na hi kriyAnirvR^ittor'tho nityo dR^iShTaH /
nityashca mokSho 'bhyupagamyate /
"eSha nityo mahimA"iti mantravarNAt /
na ca svAbhAvikAtsvabhAvAdanyannityaM kalpayituM shakyam /
svAbhAvikashcedagnyudAtmanaH svabhAvaH sa na shakyate puruShavyApArAnubhAvIti vaktum /
na hyagnerauShNyaM prakAsho vAgnuvyApArAnantarAnubhAvI /
agnivyApArAnubhAvI svAbhAvikashceti vipratiShiddham /
jvalanavyApAnAnubhAvitvamuShNaprAkAshaguNAbhyAmabhivyajyate tannAgnyepekShayA kiM tarhyanyadR^iShTeragnerauShNyaprakAshau dharmau vyavahitai kasyaciddR^iShTyA tvasaMbadhyamAnau jvalanApekShayA vyadhAnApagame dR^iShTerabhivyajyete tadapekShayA bhrAntirupajAyate jvalanapUrvakAvetAviShNaprAkAshau dharmau jAtAviti /
yadyuShNaprakAshayorapi svAbhAvikatvaM na syAt /
yaH svAbhAvaki'gnerdharmastamudAhariShyAmaH /
na ca svAbhAviko dharma eva nAsti padArthAnAmiti shakyaM vaktum /
na ca nigaDabhaN^ga ivAbhAvabhUto mokSho bandhananivR^ittirupapadyate /
paramAtmaikatvAbhyupagamAt 'ekamevAdvitIyam'iti shruteH /
na cAnyo baddho 'sti yasya nigaDanivR^ittivadbandhananivR^ittarmokShaH syAt /
paramAtmavyatirekeNAnyasyAbhAvaM vistareNAvAdiShma /
tasmAdavidyAnivR^ittimAtre mokShavyavahAra iti cAvocAma yathA rajjvAdau sarpAdyaj~nAnanivR^ittau sarpAdinivR^ittiH /
ye 'pyAcakShate mokShe vij~nAnAntaramAnandAntaraM cAbhivyajyata iti sairvaktavyo 'bhivyaktishabdArthaH /
yadi tAvatlaukikikyevopalabdhiviShayavyAptirabhivyaktishabdArthaH /
tato vaktavyaM kiM vidyamAnamabhivyajyate 'vidyamAnamiti vA /
vidyamAnaM cedyasya  muktasya tadabhivyajyate tasyA'tmabhUtameva tadityupalabdhivyavadhAnAnupapatternityAbhivyaktatvAnmuktasyAbhivyajyata iti visheShavacanamarthakam /
atha kadAcidevAbhivyajyata upalabdhivyavadhAnAdanAtmabhUtaM tadityanyato 'bhivyaktiprasaN^gaH /
tathA cAbhivyaktisAdhanApekShayA /
upalabdhisamAnAshrayatve tu vyavadhAnakalpanAnupapatteH sarvadAbhivyaktiprasaN^gaH /
tathA cAbhivyaktisAdhanApekShatA /
upalabdhisamAnAshrayatve tu vyavadhAnakalpanAnupapatteH sarvadAbhivyaktiranabhivyaktirvA /
natvantarAlakalpanAyA pramANamasti /
na ca samAnAshrayaNAmekasyA'tmabhUtAnAM dharmANAmitaretaraviShayaviShayitvaM saMbhavati /
vij~nAnasukhayoShca prAgabhivyakteH saMsAritvamabhivyaktyuttarakAlaM ca muktatvaMsya so 'nyaH parasmAnnityAbhivyaktaj~nAnasvarUpAdatyantavailakShaNyAcchaityamivauShNyAt /
paramAtmabhedakalpanAyAJNca vaidikaH kR^itAntaH parityaktaH syAt /
mokShasyedAnImiva nirvisheShatve tadarthAdhikayatnAnupapattiH shAstravaiyarthyaM ca prApnotIti cenna /
na, avidyAbhramApohApthatvAt /
na hi vastuto muktAmuktatvAvisheSho 'sti /
Atmano nityAkarUpatvAt /
kintu tadviShayAvidyApohyate shAstropadeshajanitavij~nAnena /
prAktadupadeshaprAptestadarthashca prayatna upapadyata eva /
avidyAvato 'vidyAnivR^ityanivR^ittikR^ito vesheSha AtmanaH syAditi cet /
avidyAkalpanAviShayatvAbhyupagamAdrajjUSharashuktakAgaganAnAM sarvodakarajatamalinatvAdivadadoSha ityavocAma /
timirAtimitaradR^iShTivadavidyAkartR^itvAkatR^itvAkR^ita Atmano visheShaH syAditi cet /
na /
dhyAtIva lelAyatIveti svato 'vidyAkartR^itvasva pratiShiddhatvA /
anekavyApArasannipAtajanitatvAccAvidyAbhramasya /
viShatvopapatteShca /
yasya cAvidyAbhramo ghaTAdivadvivikto gR^ihyate sa nAvidyAbhramavAn /
ahaM na jAne mugdhe 'smIti pratyatadarshanAdavidyAbhramavatvameveti cenna /
tasyApi vivekagrahaNAt /
na hi yo yasya vivekena grahItA sa tasminbhrAnta ityucyate /
tasya ca vivekagrahaNaM tasminneva ca bhrama iti vipratiShiddham /
na jAne mugdho 'smIti dR^ishyata iti bravIShi taddarshinashcAj~nAnaM mugdharUpatA dR^ishyata iti ca taddarshanasya viShayo bhavati karmatAmApadyata iti tatkathaM karmabhUtaM satkartR^isvarUpadR^ishivisheShaNaj~nAnamugdhate syAtAm /
atha dR^ishivisheShaNatvaM tayoH kathaM karma syAtAM dR^ishinA vyApyete /
karma hi kartR^ikriyayA vyApyamAnaM bhavati /
anyacca vyApyamanyadvyApakaM na tenaiva tadvyApyate /
vada kathamevaM satyaj~nAnamugdhate dR^ishivisheShaNe syAtAm /
na cAj~nAnAvivekadarshyaj~nAnamAtmanaH karmabhUtamupalabhamAna upalabdhR^idharmatvena gR^ihmAti sharIre kArshyarUpadAdavattathA /
sukhaduHkhecchAprayatnAdInsarvo loko gR^ihNAtIti cet /
tathApi grahIturlokasya vivaktataivAbhyupagatA syAt /
na jAne 'haM tvaduktaM mugdha eveti cet /
bhavatvaj~no mugdho yastvevandarshU taM j~namamugdhaM pratijAnImahe vayam /
tathA vyosenoktam /
icchAdi kR^itsnaM kShetraM kShetrI prakAshayatIti /
"samaM sarveShu bhUteShu tiShThantaM parameshvaram /
vinashyatsvavinashyantam"ityAdi shatasha uktam /
tasmAnnA'tmanaH svato baddhamuktaj~nAnakR^ito visheSho 'sti /
sarvadA samaikarasasvAbhAvyAbhyupagamAt /
ye tvato 'nyathA'tmavastu parikalpya bandhamokShAdishAstriM cArthavAdamApAdayanti ta utsahante khe 'pi shAkunaM padaM draShTuM khaM vA muShTinA'kraShTuM carmavadveShTitum /
vayaM tu tatkartumashaktAH sarvAdA samaikaramasadvaitamavikriyamajamajaramamaramamR^itamabhayamAtmatattvaM brahmaiva sma ityeSha sarvavedAntanishcitor'tha ityevaM pratipadyAmahe /
tasmAdbrahmApyetItyupacAramAtrametadvipIratagrahavaddehasaMtatervi cchedamAtraM vij~nAnaphalamapekShya //4,4.6//

START BrhUp 4,4.7

#<tad eSha shloko bhavati --
yadA sarve pramucyante kAmA ye 'sya hR^idi shritAH |
atha martyo 'mR^ito bhavaty atra brahma samashnuta iti |
tad yathAhinirlvayanI valmIke mR^itA pratyastA shayIta |
evam evedaM sharIraM shete |
athAyam asharIro 'mR^itaH prANo brahmaiva teja eva |
so 'haM bhagavate sahasraM dadAmIti hovAca janako vaidehaH || BrhUp_4,4.7 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_4,4.7 svapnabuddhAntagamanadR^iShTAntasya dArShTAntikaH saMsAro varNitaH /
saMsArahetushca vidyAkarmapUrvapraj~nA varNitA /
yaishcopAdhibhUtaiH kAryakaraNalakShaNabhUtaiH pariveShTitaH saMsAritvamanubhavati tAni coktAni /
teShAM sAkShAtprayojakau dharmAdharvAviti pUrvapakShaM kR^itvA kAma evetyavadhAritam /
yathA ca brahmaNenAyamartho 'yavadhArita evaM mantreNApIti bandhaM bandhakAraNaM coktvopasaMhR^itaM prakaraNaM"iti na kAmayamAna"iti /
athAkAyamAna ityArabhya suShuptadR^iShTanAtasya dArShTAntikabhUtaH sarvAtmabhAvo mokSha uktaH /
mokShakAraNaM cA'tmakAmatayA yadAptakAmatvamuktaM tacca sAmarthAyadanAtmaj~nAnamantareNA'tmakAmayatayA'ptakAmatvamiti sAmarthyAdbrahmavidyaiva mokShakAraNamityuktam /
ato yadyapi kAmo mUlamityuktaM tathApi mokShakAraNaviparyayeNa bandhakAraNamavidyetyedapyuktameva bhavati /

tasyaiva dR^iDhIkaraNAya mantra udAhriyate shlokashabdavAcyaH-  tattasminnevArtha eSha shloko mantro bhavati /
yadA yasminkAle sarve samastAH kAmAstR^iShNAprabhedAH pramucyante /
AtmakAmya brahmavidaH samUlato vishIryante /
ye prasiddhA loka ihAmutrArthAH putravittalokaiShaNAlakShaNA asya prasiddhasya puruShasya hR^idi buddhau shritA AshritAH /
atha tadA martyo maraNadharmA sankAmaviyogAtsamUlato 'mR^ito bhavati /
atrAsminneva sharIre vartamAno brahma samashnute brahmabhAvaM mokShaM pratipadyata ityarthaH /

tasmAdviduSho notkrAmanti prANA yAvasthitA eva svakAraNe puruShe samavanIyante /
nAmamAtraM hyavashiShyata ityuktam /
kathaM punaH samanavIteShu prANeShu dehe ca svakAraNe pralIne vidvAnmukto 'traivasarvAtmA sanvartamAnaH punaH pUrvavaddehitvaM saMsAritvalakShaNaM na pratipadyata iti /
atrocyate-tattatrAyaM dR^iShTAnto yathA loke 'hiH sarpastasya nirlvayanI nirmekaH sAhinirlvayanI valmIke sarpAshraye valmIkAdAvityarthaH /

kAmakarmaprayuktasharIrAtmabhAvena hi pUrvaM sharIro martyashca /
tadviyogAdathedAnImasharIro 'ta eva cAmR^itaH /
prANaH prANitIti prANaH /

"prANabandhanaM hi somya manaH"iti ca shrutyantare /
prakaraNavAkyasamArthAcca para evA'tmAtra prANashabdavAcyaH /
brahmaiva paramAtmaiva /
kiM punastatteja eva vij~nAnaM jyotiryenA'tmajyotiShA jagadavabhAsyamAnaM praj~nAnetraM vij~nAnajyotiShmatsadavibraMshadvartate /
yaH kAmaprashno vimokShArtho yAj~navalkyena varo datto janakAya sahetuko bandhamokShArthalakShaNo dR^iShTAntikabhUtaH sa eSha nirNItaH savistaro janakayAj~navalkyAkhyAyikArUpadhAriNyA shrutyA /
saMsAravimokShopAya uktaH prANibhyaH /
idAnIM shrutiH svayamevA'ha vidyAniShkriyArthaM janakenaivamuktamiti /
kathaM? so 'hamovaM vimokShitastvayA bhagavate tubhyaM vidyAniShkriyArthaM sahasraM dadAmIti haiva kilovAcoktavAJNjanako vaidehaH /
atra kasmdAvimokShapadArthe nirNIte videharAjyamAtmAnameva ca na nivedayatyekadeshoktAviva sahasrameva dadAti tatra ko 'bhiprAya iti /
atra kecidvarNayanti-adhyAtmavidyArasiko janakaH shrutamapyartaM punarmantraiH shushrUShati /
ato na sarvameva nivedayati /
shrutvAbhipretaM yAj~navalkyAtpunarante nivedayiShyAmIti hi manyate /

sarvamapyetadasat /

arthasheShopapatteshca /

tasmAnnA'gamanApi svargamervAdivattatpratipAdyate /
pratipAdayitrAtmabhUtaM hi tat /
pratipAdayituH pratipAdanasya pratipAdyaviShayatvAt /
bhede hi sati tadbhavati /
j~nAnaM ca tasminparAtbhAvanivR^ittireva /
na tasminsAkShAdAtmabhAvaH kartavye vidyamAnvAdAtmabhavasya /
nityo hyAtmabhAvaH sarvasyAtadviShaya iva pratyavabhasate /
tasmAdatadviShayAvabhAsanivR^ittavyatirekeNa na tasminnAtmabhAvo vidhIyate /
anyAtbhAvanivR^ittAvAtmabhAvaH svAtmani svAbhAviko yaH sa kevalo bhavatItyAtmA j~nAyata ityucyate /
svatashcAprameyaH pramANAntareNa na viShayIkriyata ityuccayate /
svatashcAprameyaH pramANAntareNa na viShayIkriyata ityubhayamapyaviruddhameva /
virajo vigatarajo rajo nAma dharmAdharmAdimalaM tadrahita ityetat /
paraH paro vyatiriktaH sUkShmo vyApI vA'kAshAdapyavyAkR^itAkhyAt /
ajo na jAyate janmapratiShedhAduttare 'pi bhAvavikArAH pratiShiddhAH /
sarveShAM janmAditvAt /
AtmA mahAnparimANato mahatatraH sarvasmAt /
dhruvo 'vinAshI //4,4.20//

#<sa vA eSha mahAn aja AtmA yo 'yaM vij~nAnamayaH prANeShu |

BrhUpBh_4,4.22 sahetukau bandhamokShAvabhihitau mantrabrAhmaNabhyAM shlokaishca punarmokShasvarUpaM vistareNa pratipAditamevametasminnAtmaviShaye sarvo vedo yathopayukto bhavati tattathA vaktavyamiti tadartheyaM kaNDikA'rabhyate /

na rAjaputravadamAtyAdibhR^ityatantraH /

no eva shAstrapriShiddhenAsAdhunA karmaNA kanIyAnalpataro bhavati pUrvAvasthAto na hIyata ityarthaH /
kiJNca sarvo hyadhiShThAnapAlanAdi kurvanparAnugrahapIDAkR^itena dharmAdharmAkhyona yujyate 'syaiva tu kathaM tadabhAva iti /
ucyate-yasmAdeSha sarveshvaraH  sankarmaNo 'pIshituM bhavatyeva shIlamasya tasmAnna karmaNA saMbandhyate /
kiJNcASha bhUtAdhipatirbrahmAdistambhaparyantAnAM bhUtAnAmadhipatirityuktArthaM padam /
eSha bhUtAnAM teShAmeva pAlayitA rakShitA /
eSha setuH /
kiMvishiShTa ityAha- vidharaNo varNAshramAdivyavasthAyA vidhArayitA /
tadAhaiShAM bhUrAdInA brahmalokAntAnAM lokAnAmasaMbhedAyAsaMbhinnamaryAdAyai /
parameshvareNa setuvadavidhAryamANA lokAH saMbhinnamaryAdAH syuH /
ato lokAnAmasaMbhedAya setubhUto 'yaM parameshvaro yaH svayaJNjyorAtmaiva /
evaMvitsarvasya vashItyAdi brahmavidyAyAH phalametannirddiShmaTam /
kijyetiriyaMpuruSha ityevamAdiShaShThaprapAThakavihitAyAmetasyAM brahmavidyAyAmevaMphalAyAM kAmyaikadeshavarjitaM kR^itsnaM karmakANDaM tAdarthyena vaniyujyate /

ke /
brAhmaNAH /
brAhmaNagrahaNamupalakShaNArtham /

sarve 'pyete yaj~navido yaj~nakShapitakalmaShAH" //
iti /
yaj~neneti dravyayaj~nA j~nAnayaj~nAshca saMskArArthAH /

kiJNcaicamevA'tmAnaM svaM lokamicchantaH prArthayantaH pravrAjinaH pravrajanashIlAH pravraDanti prakarSheNa vrajanti sarvANi karmANi saMnyasyantItyarthaH /

na hi gaN^gAdvAraM pratipitsuH kAshIdeshanivAsI pUrvAbhimukhaH praiti /
tasmAdbAhyalokatrayArthinAM putrakarmAparabrahmavidyAH sAdhanam /
"putreNAyaM loko jayyo nAnyena karmaNA" ityAdishruteH /

atatsAdhanatvAtpArivrAjyasya /

putrAdikarmaNaH AtmalokaM pratyasAdhanatvAt /
asambhavena viruddhatvamavocAma /

yathA ca bAhyalokatrayArthinaH pratiniyatAni putrAdIni sAdhanAni vihatAnyevamAtmalokArthanaH sarvaiShaNAnivR^ittiH pArivrAjyaM brahmavido vidhIyata eva /
kutaH punasta AtmalokArthanaH pravraDantyevetyucyate /
tatrArthavAdavAkyarUpeNa hotuM darshayatu /
etaddha sma vai tat /
tadetatpArivrAjye kAraNamucyate- ha sma vai kila pUrvetikrAntakAlInA vidvAMsa Atmaj~nAH prajAM karmAparabrahmavidyA ca /

nanvaparabrahmadarshamanutiShThantyeva /
tadbalAddhi vyutthAnam /
na, apavAdAt /
brahma taM parAdAdyo 'nyatrA'tmano brahma veda sarvaM taM parAdAdityaparabrahmadarshamapyapavadatyeva /

pUrvAparabAhyAntaradarshanapratiShedhAccApUrvamanaparamanantaramabAhyamiti /

sa ca bAhyaloko nAstyasmAkamAtmavyatiriktaH /

idaM me 'nenAN^gaM saMskriyata ityaN^gAN^gitvAdishravaNAt /

aviduShAM hi tatpradAjisAdhanaiH karvyaM phalam /

tasmAdAtmAnaM lokamicchantaH pravrajanti pravrajeyurityeShavidhirarthavAdena saMgacchate /

vij~nAnasamAnakartR^ikatvopadeshAdityAnAvocAma /

phalavibhAgopadeshAcca /

iShTasyArthasya saMprAptau ko vidvAnyatnamAcaret" //

iti gItAmu /

START BrhUp 4,4.23

#<tad etad R^icAbhyuktam --
eSha nityo mahimA brAhmaNasya na karmaNA vardhate no kanIyAn |
tasyaiva syAt padavittaM viditvA na lipyate karmaNA pApakeneti |
tasmAd evaMvic chAnto dAnta uparatas titikShuH samAhito bhUtvAtmany evAtmAnaM pashyati |
sarvam AtmAnaM pashyati |
nainaM pApmA tarati |
sarvaM pApmAnaM tarati |
nainaM pApmA tapati |
sarvaM pApmAnaM tapati |
vipApo virajo 'vicikitso brAhmaNo bhavati |
eSha brahmalokaH samrAT |
enaM prApito 'sIti hovAca yAj~navalkyaH |
so 'haM bhagavate videhAn dadAmi mAm cApi saha dAsyAyeti || BrhUp_4,4.23 ||>#

__________



BrhUpBh_4,4.23 tadetadvastu brAÇmaNenoktamR^icA mantreNAbhyuktaM prakAshitam /
eSha neti netyAdilakShaNo nityo mahimA /
anye tu mahimAnaH karmakR^itA ityanityAH /
ayaM tu tadvilakShaNo mahimA svAbhAvikatvAnnityo brahmavido brAhmaNasya tyaktasarveShaNasya /
kuto 'sya nityatvamiti hetumAha- karmaNA na vardhate shubhalakShaNena kR^itena vR^idvilakShaNAM vikriyAM na prApneti /
ashubhena karmaNA no kanIyAnnApyapakShayalakShaNAM vikriyAM prApnoti /
upacayApacayahetubhUtA eva hi sarvA vikriyA ityetAbhyAM pratiShidhyante /
ato 'vikriyatvAnnitya eSha mahimA /
tasmAttasyaiva mahimnaH syAdbhavetpadavitpadasya vettA padyate gamyate j~nAyata iti mahimnaH svarUpameva padaM tasya padasya veditA /
kiM tatpadavedanena syAdityucyate-taM viditvA mahimAnaM na lipyate na saMbadhyate karmaNA pApakena dharmAdharmalakShaNenobhayamapi pApakameva viduShaH /
tasmAdevamakarmasaMbandhyeSha brAhmaNasya mahimA neti netyAdilakShaNastasmAdevaMvicchAnto bAhyendriyavyApArata upashAntastathA dAnto 'ntaH karaNatR^iShNAto nivR^itta uparataH sarvaiShaNAvinirmuktaH saMnyAsI titikShurdvandvasahiShNuH samAhita indriyAntaH karaNAcalanarUpAdvyAvR^ityaikAgryarUpeNa samAhito bhUtvA /
tadetaduktaM purastAdbAlyaM ca pANDityaM ca nirvidyeti /
Atmanyeva sve kAryakaraNasaMghAta AtmAnaM pratyakcetayitAraM pashyati /
tatra kiM tAvanmAnnaM paricchinaM netyucyatesarvaM samastamAtmAnameva pashyati nAnyadAtmavyatiriktaM vAlAgramAnnamapyastItyevaM pashyati /
mananAnmunirbhavati jAgratsvapnasuShuptAkhyaM sthAnannayaM hitvA /
evaM pashyantaM brAhmaNaM nainaM pApmA puNyapApalakShaNastarati na prApneti /
ayaM tu brahmavitsarvaM pApmAnaM taratyAtmabhAvenaiva vyApnotyatikrAmati /
nainaM pApmA  kR^itAkR^italakShaNastapatIShTaphalapratyavAyotpAdanAbhyAm /
sarvaM pApmAnamayaM tapati brahmavitsarvatmadarshanavahrinA bhasmIkaroti /
sa eSha evaMvidvipAyo vigatadharmAdharmo birajo vigatarajo rajaHkAmo vigatakAmo 'vicikitsashchinnasaMshayo 'hamasmi sarvAtmA paraM brahmeti nishcitamatirbrAhmaNo bhavati /
ayaM tvevaMbhUta atasyAmavasthAyAM mukhyo brAhmaNaH prAgetasmAdbrahmasvarUpAvasthAnAdgauNamasya brAhmaNyam /
eSha brahmaloko brahmaiva loko brahmaloko mukhyo nirupacaritaH sarvAtmabhAvalakShaNo he smAraT /
enaM brahmalokaM pariprApito 'syabhayaM neti netyAdilakShaNamiti hovAca yAj~navalkyaH /
evaM brahmabhUto janako yAj~navalkyena brahmabhAvamApAditaH  pratyAha-so 'haM tvayA brahmabhAvamApAditaH sanbhagavate tubhyaM videhAndeshAnmama rAjya samastaM dadAmi mAM ca saha kartavyatAkA /
parisamAptaH paramapuruShArthaH /
etAvatpuruSheNa kartavyameShA niShThaiShA parA gatiretanniHshreyasametatprApya kR^itakR^ityo brAhmaNo bhavatyetatsarvavedAnushAsanamiti //4,4.23//

BrhUpBh_4,4.25 idAnIM samastasyaivA'raNyarakasya yor'tha uktaH sa samuccityAsyA kaNDikAyAM nirdishyata  etAvAnsamastAraNyakArtha iti /

START BrhUp 4,5.1

#<atha ha yAj~navalkyasya dve bhArye babhUvatur maitreyI ca kAtyAyanI ca |

BrhUpBh_4,5.1 AgamapradhAnena madhukANDena brahmatattvaM nirdhAritam /

START BrhUp 4,5.15

#<yatra hi dvaitam iva bhavati tad itara itaraM pashyati, tad itara itaraM jighrati, tad itara itaraM rasayate, tad itara itaram abhivadati, tad itara itaraM shR^iNoti, tad itara itaraM manute. tad itara itaraM spR^ishati, tad itara itaraM vijAnAti |

BrhUpBh_4,5.15 caturShvapi prapAThakeShveka AtmA tulyo nirdhAritaH paraM brahma /
upAyavisheShastu tasyAdhigame 'nyashcAnyashca /
upeyastu sa evA'tmA yashcaturthe 'thAta Adesho neti netIti nirdiShTaH /

punaH paJNcamasamAptau /
punarjanakayAj~navalkyasaMvAde /
punarihopaniShatsamAptau /
caturNAmapi prapAThakAnAmetadAtmaniShThatA nAnyo 'ntarAle kashcidapi vivakShiter'tha ityetatpradarshanAyAnta upasaMhAraH sa eSha neti netyAdiH /
yasmAtprakArashatenApi nirUpyamANe tattave neti netyAtmaiva niShThA nAnyopalabhyate tarkeNa vA'gamena vA tasmAdetadevAmR^itatvasAdhanaM yadetanneti netyAtmaparij~nAnaM sarvasaMnyAsashcetyetamarthamupasaMjihIrShannAha-etAvadetAvanmAtraM  yadetanneti netyadvaitAtmadarshanamidaM cAnyasahakArikAraNanirapekShamevAre maitreyyamR^itatvasAdhanam /
yatpR^iShTatyasi yadeva bhagavAnveda tadeva me brUhyamR^itatvasAdhanamiti tadetAvadevetu vij~neyaM tvayeti haivaM kilAmR^itatvasAdhanamAtmaj~nAnaM priyAyai bhAryAyA uktvA saMnyAsaparyavasAnA /
etAvAnupadesha etadvedAnushAsanameShA paramaniShThaiSha puruShArthakartavyatAnta iti /
idAnIM vicAryate shAstrArthavivekapratipattaye /
yata AkulAni hi vAkyAni dR^ishyante"yAvajjIvamagnihotraM juhuyAt" "yAvajjIvaM darshapUrNamAsAbhyAM yajeta" "kurvanneveha karmANi jijIviShecchataM samAH" "etadvai jarAmaryaM sarvaM yadagnihotram"ityAdInyaikAshramyAj~nApakAnyAni cA'shramAntarapratipAdakAni vAkyAni"viditvA vyutthAya pravrajanti" "brahmacaryaM samApya gR^ihI bhavedgrahAdvanI bhUtvA pravrajet" "yadi vetarathA brahmacaryAdeva pravrajedgR^ihAdvA vanAdvA"iti /
"na karmaNA na prajayA dhanena tyAgenaikemR^itatvamAnashuH"ityAdIni /
tathA smR^itayashca-"brahmacaryavAnpravrajati" "avishIrNabrahmacaryo yamicchattamAvaseti"tasyA'shramamavikalpamekebruvate"tathA-"vaidAnanadhItya brahmacaryeNa putrapautrAnicchetpAvanArthaM pitR^iNAm /
agnInAdhAya vidhivacceShTayaj~no vanaM pravishyAtha munirbubhUShet" //
"prAjApatyAM nirupyeShTiM sarvavesadakShiNAm /
AtmanyagnInsamAropya brAhmaNaH pravrajedgR^ihAt" //
ityAdyAH /
evaM vyutthAnavikalpakramayateShTAshramapratipattipratApAdakAni hi shrutismR^itivAkyAni shatasha upalaMbhyanta itaretaraviruddhAni /
AcArashca tadvidAm /
vipratipattishca shAstrArthapratapattÌNAM bahuvidAmapi /
ato na shakyate shAstrArtho mandabuddhibhirvivekena pratipattum /
pariniShThatashAstranyAyabuddhibhireva hyoShAM vAkyAnAM viShayavibhAgaH shakyate 'vadhArayitum /
tasmAdeShAM viShayavibhAgaj~nApanAya yathAbuddhisAmarthaMya vicArayiShyAmaH /
yAvajjIvashrutyAdivAkyAnAmanyArthAsaMbhavAtkriyAvasAna ava vedArtha /
taM yaj~napAtrairdahantItyantyakarmashravaNAjjarAmaryashravaNAcca liN^gAcca bhasmAntaM sharIramiti /
na hi pArivrAjyapakShe bhasmAntatA sharIrasya syAt /
smR^itishca-"niShekAdishmashAnAnto mantrairyasyodito vidhiH /
tasyA shAstre 'dhikAro 'smiJNj~neyo nAnyasya kasyacit"iti /
samantrakaM hi yatkarma vedeneha vidhIyate tasya shmashAnAntatAM darshayati smR^itiH /
adhikArAbhAvapradarshanAccAtyantameva shrutyadhikArAbhAvo 'karmiNo gamyate /
agnyudvAsanApavAdAcca 'vIrahA vA eSha devAnAM yo 'gnimudvAsayate' iti /
nanu vyutthAnAdivijhadhAnAdvaikalpikaM kriyAvasAnatvaM vedArthasya /
na /
anyArthatvAdvyutthAnAdishrutInAm /
'yAvajjIvamannihotraM juhoti'"yAjjIvaM darshapUrNamAsAbhyAM yajeta"ityevamAdInAM shrutInAM jIvanamAtranimittatvAdyadA na shakyate 'nyArthatA kalpayituM tadA vyutthAnAdivAkyAnAM karmAnadhikR^itaviShayatvasaMbhavAt /
"kurvanneveha karmANi jijIvaShecchataM samAH"iti ca mantravarNAjjarayA vA hyevAsmAnmucyate mR^ityunA veti ca jarAmR^ityubhyAmanyatra karmaviyogAcchidrAsaMbhavAtkarmiNAM shmashAnAntatvaM na vaikalpikam /
kANakubjAdayo 'pi karmaNyanadhikR^itA anugrAhyA eva shrutyeti vyutthAnAdyAshramAntaravidhAnaM nAnupapannam /
pArivrAjyAkramavidhAnasyAnavakAshatvamiti cet /
na /
vishvajitsarvamedhayoryAvajjIvavidhyapavAdatvAt /
yAvajjIvAgnihotrAdividhervishvajitsarvamedhayorevApavAdastatra ca kramapratipattisaMbhavo"brahmacaryaM samApya gR^ihI bhavedgR^ihAdvanI bhutvA pravrajedi"ti  virodhAnupapatteH /
na hyevaMviShayatve pArivrAjyakamavidhAnavAkyasya kashcidvirodhaH kramapratipatteH /
anyaviShayaparikalpanAyAM kashcidbAdhaH /
nA'tmaj~nAnasyAmR^itatvahetutvAbhyupagamAt /
yattAvadAtmetyevopAsItetyArabhya sa eSha neti netyetadantena granthena yadupasaMhR^itamAtmaj~nAnaM tadamR^itatvasAdhanamityabhyupagataM bhavatA /
tatraitAvadevAmR^itatvasAdhanamanyanirapekShamityetanna mR^iShyate /
tatra bhavantaM pR^icchAmi kimarthamAtmaj~nAnaM marShayati bhavAniti /
shR^iNu tatra kAraNaM yathAsvargakAmasya svargaprAptyupAyamajAnato 'gnihotrAdi svargasAdhanamabhyupagamyate tathehApyAtmaj~nAnam /
yathA j~nApyate tatAbhUtamevAmR^itatvasAdhanamAtmaj~nAnamabhyupagantuM yuktam tulyaprAmANyAdubhayatra /
yadyevaM kiM syAt /
sarvakarmahetUpamardakatvAdAtmaj~nAnasya vidyodbhave karmanivR^ittiH syAt /
dArAgnisaMbaddhAnAM tAvadagnihotrAdikarmaNAM bhedabuddhiviShayasaMpradAnakArakasAdhyatvam /
anyabuddhiparacchedyAM hyagnyAdidevatAM saMpradAnakArakabhUtAmantreNa na hi tatkarma nirvartyate /
yayA hi saMpradAnakArakabuddhyA saMpradAnakArakaM karmasAdhanatvenopadishyate seha vidyayA nivartyate"anyo 'sAvanyo 'hamasmIti na sa veda" "devAstaM parAduryo 'nyatrA'tmano devAnveda" "mR^ityo sa mR^ityumApnoti ya iha nAneva pashyati" "ekadhaivAnudraShTavyaM sarvamAtmAnaM pashyati"ityAdishrutibhyaH /
na ca deshakAlanimitta dyapekShatvaM vyavasthitAtmavastuviShayatvAdAtmaj~nAnasya /
kriyAyAstu puruShatantratvAtsyAddeshakAlanimittAdyepekShatvam /
j~nAnaM tu vastutantratvAnna deshakAlanimittAdyapekShate /
yathAgniruShNa AkAsho 'mUrta iti tathA'tmavij~nAnamapu /
nanvevaM sati prAmANabhUtasya karvidhernirodhaH syAt /
na ca tulyapramANayoritaretaranirodho yuktaH /
na /
svAbhAvikabhedabuddhimAtranirodhakatvAt /
na hi vidhyantaranirodhakamAtmaj~nAnam svAbhAvikabhedabuddhimAtraM niruNaddhi /
tathApi hetvapahArAtkarmAnupapattervidhainirodha eva syAditi cet /
na /
kAmapratiShedhAtkAmyapravR^ittinirodhavadadoShAt /
yathA svargakAmo yajeteti svargasAdhane yAge pravR^ittasya kAmapratiShevidheH kAme vihate kAmyayAgAnuShThAnapravR^ittirnirudhyate /
na caitAvatA kAmyavidhirniruddho bhavati /
kAmapratiShedhavidhinA kAmyavidheranarkatvaj~nAnAtpravR^ityanupapattiriti cet /
ananuShTheyatve 'nuShThAturabhAvAdanuShThAnavidhyAnarthakyAdaprAmANyameva karmavidhInAmiti cet /
na /
prAgAtmaj~nAnAtpravR^ityupapatteH svAbhAvikasya kriyAkArakaphalabhedavij~nAnasya prAgAtmaj~nAnAtkarmahetutvamupapadyata eva /
yathA kAmaviShaye doShavij~nAnotpatteH prAkkAmyakarmapravR^ittihetutvaM syAdeva svargAdIcchAyAH svAbhAvikyAstadvAt /
tathA satyanarthArtho veda iti cet /
na /
arthAnarthayorabhiprAtatantratvAt /
mokShamekaM varjayitvAnyasyAvidyAviShayatvAta /
puruShAbhiprAyatantrau hyArthAnarthau /
maraNAdikAmyeShTadarshanAt /
tasmAdyAvadAtmaj~nAnavidherAbhimukhyaM tAvadeva karmavidhaya /
tasmAnnA'tmaj~nAnasahabhAvitvaM karmaNAmityataH siddhamAtmaj~nAnamevAmR^itatvasAdhanametAvadare khalvamR^itatvamiti /
karmanirapekShatvAjj~nAnasya /
ato viduShastAvatpArivrAjyaM  siddhaM saMpradAnAdikarmakArakajAtyAdishUnyAvikriyabrahmAtmadR^iDhapratipattimAtreNa vacanamantareNApyuktanyAyataH /
tathAca vyAkhyAtametat"yeShAM no 'yamAtmAyaM loka"iti hotuvacanena /
pUrve vidvAsaH prajAmakAmayamAnA vyuttiShThantIti pArivrAjyaM viduShAmAtmalokAvabodhAdeva /
tathAca vividiShorapu siddhaM pArivrAjyam /
"etamevA'tmAnaM lokamicchantaH pravrajanti"iti vacanAt /
karmaNAM cAvidvadviShayatvamavocAma /
avidyAviShaye cotpatyAptivikArasaMskArthAni karmANItyataH AtmasaMskAradvaireNA'tmaj~nAnasAdhanatvamapi karmaNAmavocAma yaj~nAdibhirvividaShantIti /
athaita satyavidviShayANAmAshramakarmaNAM balAbalavicAraNAyAmAtmaj~nAnotpAdanaM prati yamapradhAnAnAmamAnitvAdInAM mAnasAnAM ca dhyAnaj~nAnavairAgyAdInAM sannipatyopakAratvam /
hiMsArAgadveShAdibAhulyAdbahukliShTakarmavimishritA itara ityataH pArivrAjyaM mumukShUNAM prashaMsanti-"tyAga eva hi sarveShAmuktAnAmapi karmaNAm /
vairAgyaM punaretasya mokShasya paramo 'vadhiH" //
"kiM te dhanena kimu bandhubhiste kiM te dArairbrAhmaNa yo mariShyasi /
AtmAnamanviccha guhA praviShTaM pitAmahAste kva gatAH pitA ca //
"evaM sAkhyayogashAstreShu ca saMnyAso j~nAnaM prati pratyAsanna ucyate /
kAmapravR^ittyabhAvAcca /
kAmapravR^itterhi j~nAnapratikUlatA sarvashAstreShu prasiddhA /
tasmAdviraktasya mumukShorvinApi j~nAnena brahmacaryAdeva pravrajedityAdyUpapannam /
nanu sAvakAshatvAdanadhikR^itaviShayametadityuktaM yAvajjIvashrutyuparodhAt /
naiSha doShaH /
nitarAM sAvakAshatvAdyAvajjIvashrutInAm /
avadvitkAmikartavyatA hyavocAma sarvakarmaNAm /
na tu nirapekShameva jIvananimittameva kartavyaM karma /
prAyeNahi puruShAH kAmabahulAH /
kAmashcAnekaviShayo 'nekakarmasAdhanasAdhyashca /
anekaphalasAdhanAni ca vaidikAni  karmANi dArAgnisaMbandhapuruShakartavyAnu punaH punashcAnuShThIyamAnAnu bahuphalAnu kR^iShyAdivadvarShashatasamAptIni ca gArhasthye vAraNye vAtastadapekShayA yAvajjIvashrutayaH /
'kurvanneveha karmANi' iti ca mantravarNaH /
tasmiMshca pakShe vishvajitsarvamedhayoH karmaparityAgaH /
yasmiMshca pakShe yAvajjIvAnuShThAnaM tadA shmashAnAntatvaM bhasmAntatA ca sharIrasya /
itaravarNApekShayA vA yAvajjIvashrutiH /
na hi kShattriyavaishyayo pArivrAjyapratipattirasti /
tathA 'mantrairyasyodito vidhiH' /
'aikAshramyaM tvAcAryA' ityevamAdInAM kShatriyavaishyApekShatvam /
tasmAtpurushasAmarthayaj~nAnavairAgyakAmAdyapekShayA vyutthAnavikalpakramapArivrAjyapripattaprakArA na virudhyante /
anadhikR^itAnAM ca pR^ithagvidhAnAtpArivrAjyas 'snAtako vAsnAtako votsannAgniranagniko ve'tyAdinA /
tasmAtsiddhAshramAntarANyadhikR^itAnAmeva //4,5.15//

iti paJNcamaM brAhmaNam //
